        <a class="extiw" href="https://pt.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jana%C3%ADna_Paschoal" title="pt:Janaína Paschoal">
         pt
        </a>
        )
       </span>
       and Miguel Reale Junior; Rousseff was represented by her lawyer, José Eduardo Cardozo.
      </p>
      <table class="cquote pullquote" role="presentation" style="float:right; border-collapse: collapse; border: none; background-color: transparent; width: 25%;">
       <tr>
        <td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: top; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: left; padding: 10px 10px;">
         “
        </td>
        <td style="vertical-align: top; border: none; padding: 4px 10px;">
         <small>
          Fraud is the will to, free and consciously, to practice the misconduct and get the result. And that's what the President did. She edited the decrees by a free and conscious mode to increase costs, that could not increased by a decree. She should send a
          <a href="/wiki/Bill_(law)" title="Bill (law)">
           bill
          </a>
          .
         </small>
        </td>
        <td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: bottom; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: right; padding: 10px 10px;">
         ”
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td class="cquotecite" colspan="3" style="border: none; padding-right: 4%; font-size: smaller; text-align: right;">
         <cite>
          — Julio Marcelo de Oliveira,
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Federal_Court_of_Accounts" title="Federal Court of Accounts">
           Federal Court of Accounts
          </a>
          (TCU), Agência Brasil.
          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JMO_115-0">
           <a href="#cite_note-JMO-115">
            [115]
           </a>
          </sup>
         </cite>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <p>
       Oliveira, procurator of the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Federal_Court_of_Accounts" title="Federal Court of Accounts">
        Federal Court of Accounts
       </a>
       (TCU), said that in April 2015 TCU identified the recidivist fiscal misconduct, so-called "tax pedaling", immediately rejected. There was no previous understanding to modify the rules and the consensus, and every time that the TCU has ruled, it had disapproved the conduct adopted by Rousseff.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JMO_115-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-JMO-115">
         [115]
        </a>
       </sup>
       He reiterated that the President acted intentionally to borrow from public banks, and acted "coercively" in these operations. This, in his opinion, was serious, and forbidden by the fiscal responsibility law. The practice, he said, went on for years, including throughout the year 2015.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116">
        <a href="#cite_note-116">
         [116]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Antonio Carlos Costa D'avila Carvalho, the auditor of TCU, said that the Rousseff's fiscal practices were unprecedented and caused serious outcomes.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-117">
        <a href="#cite_note-117">
         [117]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Adriano Pereira de Paula, credit operations manager of the National Treasury, and Otavio Ladeira de Medeiros, deputy secretary of the National Treasury, also testified during this session.
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify">
          <span title="The text near this tag may need clarification or removal of jargon. (May 2017)">
           clarification needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Prosecution witnesses Tiago Alves de Gouveia Lins Dutra and Leonardo Rodrigues Albernaz, both TCU auditors, testified on 13 June. Tiago Dutra said that Rousseff created overdrafts with public banks in 2015 that had already observed in 2014. A TCU report indicated a delay of eleven months in transferring to banks an amount of R$2.6 billion, and five months in transferring R$3 billion related to the operations. For principal and interest, until December 2015, the government have been paid R$15 billion, of which R$2 billion were related to interest.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-118">
        <a href="#cite_note-118">
         [118]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Albernaz said that more than fifty auditors had carried out an analysis of Rousseff accounts and concluded unanimously that her administration has made "the most reckless management" of public finances since the Fiscal Responsibility Law was enacted in May 2000.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-119">
        <a href="#cite_note-119">
         [119]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Committee President
       <a href="/wiki/Raimundo_Lira" title="Raimundo Lira">
        Raimundo Lira
       </a>
       announced the decision of the President of the Supreme Court, Ricardo Lewandowski, authorizing an audit requested by the defense. Lira designated a board consisting of three experts, granting to prosecution, defense and Senators 48 hours to formulate questions and indicate technical assistants, as well as 24 hours to refute the appointed experts, fixing also a ten-day deadline for the completion of the audit.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-120">
        <a href="#cite_note-120">
         [120]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <table class="cquote pullquote" role="presentation" style="float:right; border-collapse: collapse; border: none; background-color: transparent; width: 25%;">
       <tr>
        <td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: top; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: left; padding: 10px 10px;">
         “
        </td>
        <td style="vertical-align: top; border: none; padding: 4px 10px;">
         <small>
          I don't understand that it was a credit operation, but a rendering of services. At no time that the Union [Government] pays to bank was directly related to what the
          <a href="/wiki/Producer_(agriculture)" title="Producer (agriculture)">
           producers
          </a>
          has received. The producers received from the bank itself. The Union participation doesn't characterize a credit operation between the Union and public banks.
         </small>
        </td>
        <td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: bottom; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: right; padding: 10px 10px;">
         ”
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td class="cquotecite" colspan="3" style="border: none; padding-right: 4%; font-size: smaller; text-align: right;">
         <cite>
          — Gilson Bittencourt, former National Secretary of Planning and Strategic Investment, Agência Brasil.
          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GB_121-0">
           <a href="#cite_note-GB-121">
            [121]
           </a>
          </sup>
         </cite>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <p>
       On 14 June, the first defense witnesses testified. They were former Secretary of Planning and Strategic Investment, Gilson Bittencourt, and former Secretary of Agricultural Policy of the
       <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Agriculture_(Brazil)" title="Ministry of Agriculture (Brazil)">
        Ministry of Agriculture
       </a>
       , André Nassar. Bittencourt said that there was no credit operation between the Government and public banks and also denied that there was a delay in paying interest to public banks in 2015. According to him, the debit to be paid in 2016 came due only at the time of collection by the banks, every six months.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GB_121-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-GB-121">
         [121]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Nassar said that the Bank of Brazil had an interest in "circulating money", by lending to producers, and even in getting the transfers delayed by the government. He also said that, as Secretary of Agricultural Policy and from the point of view of the agricultural sector, this was important to avoid a disruption that, had it occurred, would have generated serious outcomes to the sector.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-122">
        <a href="#cite_note-122">
         [122]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       On 15 June, former Deputy Secretary of the Federal Budget Office, Cilair Rodrigues de Abreu, former Secretary of Budget and Administration for the
       <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Social_Security" title="Ministry of Social Security">
        Ministry of Social Security
       </a>
       , José Geraldo França Diniz, and Consultant for the Ministry of Planning, Budget, and Management, Walter Baere de Araújo Filho, all testified. Rodrigues said that the understanding of the TCU before 2015 had always been that the future target could be used by the budget secretary in the publication of their reports. This understanding did not change, he said, until 2015.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-123">
        <a href="#cite_note-123">
         [123]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Diniz testified that due to the complexity of supplemental budget decrees, the documents are reviewed by experts and that while Rousseff signed, it would have been impossible for herself to analyze in detail 200 pages of attachments, calculations and spreadsheets. Walter Baere said that the TCU had never issued a formal opinion concerning the illegality of supplemental budget decrees by the President, and that the TCU had the specific legal duty to raise an alert whenever there is a possibility of the non-attainment of fiscal targets.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-124">
        <a href="#cite_note-124">
         [124]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Former Executive Secretary of the
       <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Education_(Brazil)" title="Ministry of Education (Brazil)">
        Ministry of Education
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Luiz_Cl%C3%A1udio_Costa&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Luiz Cláudio Costa (page does not exist)">
        Luiz Cláudio Costa
       </a>
       <span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">
        (
        <a class="extiw" href="https://pt.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luiz_Cl%C3%A1udio_Costa" title="pt:Luiz Cláudio Costa">
         pt
        </a>
        )
       </span>
       , former Assistant Executive Secretary of the Ministry of Education, Wagner Vilas Boas, Assistant Secretary of Planning and Budget of the Ministry of Education, Iara Ferreira Pinho, and Director of the Department of Economic Programs of the Secretary of Federal Budget, Clayton Luiz Montes, all testified on 16 June. According to Luiz Claudio Costa, the supplemental budget decree for the Ministry of Education
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-125">
        <a href="#cite_note-125">
         [125]
        </a>
       </sup>
       was important for the management, enabling several sectors linked to the Ministry, such as universities, institutes and others, to ensure their budget met immediate needs.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-126">
        <a href="#cite_note-126">
         [126]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Vilas Boas explained that it was not appropriate for the Ministry of Education to evaluate the impact of the credit opening for obtaining the primary balance target. He said that the sectorial authority – in this case the agencies of the Ministry – makes a request for supplemental budget, but that this is subject to policy guidance and technical supervision by the budget agency. Both, Wagner Vilas Boas and Iara Pinho, said they could not give an opinion on the compatibility of the signed supplementary decrees and the current fiscal target since their functions don't allow them to conduct an analysis of the achievement of the target. Concerning these statements, the prosecution pointed out that the technicians were not able to explain specifically the possible crime of responsibility. "The witnesses left show that they are unaware the facts. Our claim is that the evidence shall be excused," said prosecution lawyer, Janaina Paschoal, after the testimony of Iara Pinho.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127">
        <a href="#cite_note-127">
         [127]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-128">
        <a href="#cite_note-128">
         [128]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Clayton Luiz Montes said that "the government has followed the new understanding of the TCU by October 2015. Since that time, we were not sent any credit decrees".
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-129">
        <a href="#cite_note-129">
         [129]
        </a>
       </sup>
       This, nevertheless, conflicted with the statements of TCU auditors—that there was no previous understanding to modify the rules.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JMO_115-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-JMO-115">
         [115]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       On 17 June, former Minister of Planning, Budget and Management,
       <a href="/wiki/Nelson_Barbosa" title="Nelson Barbosa">
        Nelson Barbosa
       </a>
       , former Minister of Education,
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Jos%C3%A9_Henrique_Paim&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="José Henrique Paim (page does not exist)">
        José Henrique Paim
       </a>
       <span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">
        (
        <a class="extiw" href="https://pt.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Henrique_Paim" title="pt:José Henrique Paim">
         pt
        </a>
        )
       </span>
       , Director of the Department of Infrastructure Programs of the Federal Budget Secretary, Zarak de Oliveira Ferreira, Analyst of Planning and Budget of the Ministry of Planning, Budget and Management, Antonio José Chatack Carmelo, and Planning and Budget Analyst of the Federal Budget Office, Georgimar Martiniano de Sousa, testified. Nelson Barbosa said that the additional credit decrees issued by President Rousseff from June to August 2015 did not prevent the fulfillment of the fiscal target approved by Congress in early 2015 and, since it was a supplemental credit that had no impact on the target, was not considered a target of primary balance, but to give more autonomy to the allocation of a value already available.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-130">
        <a href="#cite_note-130">
         [130]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Henrique Paim said that the decrees were essential to the functioning of various sectors of Education, including scientific research and operation of universities. Moreover, according to the former minister, the additional credits are often edited based on revenue generation, provided by "budget units", linked to the Ministry.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-131">
        <a href="#cite_note-131">
         [131]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Also the technicians Zarak de Oliveira, Chatack Carmelo and Georgimar Martiniano, have not seen incompatibility of supplemental decrees with the fiscal target.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-132">
        <a href="#cite_note-132">
         [132]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       From 20 to 24 June, there were five meetings, with hearings of fifteen witnesses called by the defense.
      </p>
      <p>
       On 20 June, former Deputy Chief for Legal Affairs of
       <a href="/wiki/Chief_of_Staff_of_Brazil" title="Chief of Staff of Brazil">
        Staff of the Presidency
       </a>
       Ivo da Motta Azevedo Correa, former Minister of Education
       <a href="/wiki/Renato_Janine_Ribeiro" title="Renato Janine Ribeiro">
        Renato Janine Ribeiro
       </a>
       Director of the Department of Social Programs of the Secretary of Federal Budget Felipe Daruich Neto, and former Deputy Executive Secretary of the Staff of the Presidency Bruno Moretti, all testified. Ivo Correa said that an alert of the TCU was not a decision of the Court, and thus, the government relied on previous jurisprudence to edit the decrees. Janine Ribeiro said that no alert was received from the TCU about irregularities in the supplemental budget decrees when Minister of Education.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-133">
        <a href="#cite_note-133">
         [133]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Daruich Neto said that, at no time was there any intentional misconduct and that it was impracticable for the President to evaluate all decrees before signing them.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-134">
        <a href="#cite_note-134">
         [134]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Former Minister of the
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Secretary_of_Human_Rights&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Secretary of Human Rights (page does not exist)">
        Secretary of Human Rights
       </a>
       <span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">
        (
        <a class="extiw" href="https://pt.wikipedia.org/wiki/Secretaria_de_Direitos_Humanos_da_Presid%C3%AAncia_da_Rep%C3%BAblica" title="pt:Secretaria de Direitos Humanos da Presidência da República">
         pt
        </a>
        )
       </span>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Pepe_Vargas&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Pepe Vargas (page does not exist)">
        Pepe Vargas
       </a>
       <span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">
        (
        <a class="extiw" href="https://pt.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pepe_Vargas" title="pt:Pepe Vargas">
         pt
        </a>
        )
       </span>
       , former Minister of Planning, Budget and Management
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Miriam_Belchior&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Miriam Belchior (page does not exist)">
        Miriam Belchior
       </a>
       <span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">
        (
        <a class="extiw" href="https://pt.wikipedia.org/wiki/Miriam_Belchior" title="pt:Miriam Belchior">
         pt
        </a>
        )
       </span>
       (who was also the former President of Caixa Econômica Federal), Planning and Budget Analyst Orlando Magalhães da Cunha, and Coordinator of Budget and Finance of the Ministry of Justice Marcelo Minghelli, testified on 21 June. The former Minister Pepe Vargas asserted that the supplemental credit to the Secretary of Human Rights was derived not just from treasury resources, but from surplus funds obtained through donations by individuals and corporations.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-135">
        <a href="#cite_note-135">
         [135]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Mirian Belchior said that the supplemental budget decrees, by which Rousseff was indicted were lawful and that it was impossible to increase the budgetary contingency that was made in 2015.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136">
        <a href="#cite_note-136">
         [136]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Planning and Budget Analyst and General Coordinator of Technology and Information of the Federal Budget Office Robson Azevedo Rung, Secretary of Institutional Organization of the
       <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Defence_(Brazil)" title="Ministry of Defence (Brazil)">
        Ministry of Defence
       </a>
       Luiz Antonio de Souza Cordeiro, and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Superior_Labor_Court" title="Superior Labor Court">
        Superior Labor Court
       </a>
       representative Luciano Carlos de Almeida testified on 22 June. Azevedo Rung said that the Federal Budget Office received a new interpretation from TCU only in 2015, concerning the procedures that were ever well settled.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137">
        <a href="#cite_note-137">
         [137]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Also at this session, the Committee approved a new
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Timetable" title="Timetable">
        timetable
       </a>
       for the trial – on 6 July, the testimony of Rousseff, who could be represented by her lawyer, José Eduardo Cardozo; from 7 to 12 July, final arguments of the prosecution; and from 13 to 27 July, final arguments of the defence. On 9 August, there was to be discussion and voting on the report in plenary; and 22 August was the estimated date for the final judgement.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138">
        <a href="#cite_note-138">
         [138]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139">
        <a href="#cite_note-139">
         [139]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:CEI_2016_23_June_2016.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3456" data-file-width="5184" height="167" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/CEI_2016_23_June_2016.jpg/250px-CEI_2016_23_June_2016.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/CEI_2016_23_June_2016.jpg/375px-CEI_2016_23_June_2016.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/CEI_2016_23_June_2016.jpg/500px-CEI_2016_23_June_2016.jpg 2x" width="250"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:CEI_2016_23_June_2016.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <center>
          Committee meeting on 23 June 2016
         </center>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The Deputy Secretary of Planning, Budget and Administration of the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Science,_Technology_and_Innovation_(Brazil)" title="Ministry of Science, Technology and Innovation (Brazil)">
        Ministry of Science, Technology and Innovation
       </a>
       Anderson Lozi da Rocha and former Federal Budget Secretary Esther Dweck testified on 23 June. Dweck denied that the supplemental budget decrees in 2015 had contributed to the breach of the target for primary surplus for that year.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140">
        <a href="#cite_note-140">
         [140]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Two more witnesses (former Executive Secretary of the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Labor_and_Employment_(Brazil)" title="Ministry of Labor and Employment (Brazil)">
        Ministry of Labor and Employment
       </a>
       Francisco José Pontes Ibiapina and the Director of Special Programs of the Secretary of Federal Budget Marcos de Oliveira Ferreira) testified on 24 June. Pontes Ibiapina said that the supplemental budget decrees were published to aid programs such as the transfer of resources to States and Municipalities, by the
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=National_Employment_System&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="National Employment System (page does not exist)">
        National Employment System
       </a>
       <span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">
        (
        <a class="extiw" href="https://pt.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sistema_Nacional_de_Emprego" title="pt:Sistema Nacional de Emprego">
         pt
        </a>
        )
       </span>
       and other programs.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141">
        <a href="#cite_note-141">
         [141]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Former
       <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Agrarian_Development_(Brazil)" title="Ministry of Agrarian Development (Brazil)">
        Ministry of Agrarian Development
       </a>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Patrus_Ananias&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Patrus Ananias (page does not exist)">
        Patrus Ananias
       </a>
       <span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">
        (
        <a class="extiw" href="https://pt.wikipedia.org/wiki/Patrus_Ananias" title="pt:Patrus Ananias">
         pt
        </a>
        )
       </span>
       testified on 27 June. Ananias said that he did not acknowledge the "tax pedalling" and the resources were transferred from the Bank of Brazil directly to producers at subsidized interest rates, due to the attention that agriculture deserved.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142">
        <a href="#cite_note-142">
         [142]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       On 28 June were heard
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Maria_Fernanda_Ramos_Coelho&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Maria Fernanda Ramos Coelho (page does not exist)">
        Maria Fernanda Ramos Coelho
       </a>
       <span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">
        (
        <a class="extiw" href="https://pt.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maria_Fernanda_Ramos_Coelho" title="pt:Maria Fernanda Ramos Coelho">
         pt
        </a>
        )
       </span>
       , former Executive Secretary of the Ministry of Agrarian Development;
       <a href="/wiki/Aldo_Rebelo" title="Aldo Rebelo">
        Aldo Rebelo
       </a>
       , former Ministry of Defence;
       <a href="/wiki/Lu%C3%ADs_In%C3%A1cio_Adams" title="Luís Inácio Adams">
        Luís Inácio Adams
       </a>
       , former
       <a href="/wiki/Attorney_General_of_Brazil" title="Attorney General of Brazil">
        General's Office attorney
       </a>
       ; and Antônio Carlos Stangherlin Rebelo, who was responsible for analysis of supplemental credits on the
       <a href="/wiki/National_Justice_Council" title="National Justice Council">
        National Justice Council
       </a>
       . Maria Fernanda said that the delay in the payment of interest rate equalization of the Plan Safra (government's plan to support agriculture) for 2015, did not configure a credit operation, since the non-compliance was not subject to penalty payment in the contract terms. According to former Secretary, the values were only monetarily adjusted. The prosecution lawyer Janaína Paschoal rejected the claims of Maria Fernanda and said that the remuneration per
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Interest_rate_SELIC&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Interest rate SELIC (page does not exist)">
        interest rate SELIC
       </a>
       <span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">
        (
        <a class="extiw" href="https://pt.wikipedia.org/wiki/taxa_SELIC" title="pt:taxa SELIC">
         pt
        </a>
        )
       </span>
       (a benchmark interest rate of the Brazilian economy) is a proof that there was a credit operation. The prosecution reiterated that this statement confirmed the infringement materially, she concluded.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-143">
        <a href="#cite_note-143">
         [143]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Aldo Rebelo rejected the accusations that the government spent wantonly in 2015, and that year was characterized by fiscal adjustments and efforts to reduce public spending.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-144">
        <a href="#cite_note-144">
         [144]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       On 29 June were heard João Luiz Guadagnin, Director of the Department of Finance and Production Protection of the Ministry of Agrarian Development; Marcel Mascarenhas dos Santos, Prosecutor of the
       <a href="/wiki/Central_Bank_of_Brazil" title="Central Bank of Brazil">
        Central Bank
       </a>
       ; Fernando Rocha, Deputy Head of the Economic Department of the Central Bank; and Paulo José dos Reis Souza, Finance and Control Analyst and Fiscal Policy Secretary on the
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=National_Treasury_Secretary&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="National Treasury Secretary (page does not exist)">
        National Treasury Secretary
       </a>
       <span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">
        (
        <a class="extiw" href="https://pt.wikipedia.org/wiki/Secretaria_do_Tesouro_Nacional" title="pt:Secretaria do Tesouro Nacional">
         pt
        </a>
        )
       </span>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-145">
        <a href="#cite_note-145">
         [145]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-final_hearings_146-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-final_hearings-146">
         [146]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The witness hearings ended on 29 June. A total of 44 witnesses were heard, six convened by prosecution and 38 by the defense. At the end of the witnesses hearings phase, both the prosecution and the defense lawyers said they were confident of their respective theses. Prosecution lawyer Janaina Paschoal criticized the actions of Rousseff's defense because of the large number of witnesses called. Defense lawyer José Eduardo Cardozo also expressed confidence, but said that the process had political undertones and that this might interfere with the result. He also pointed out that some senators refused to question the witnesses because there was already a predetermined outcome prior to the completion of work.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-final_hearings_146-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-final_hearings-146">
         [146]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h4>
       <span id="Auditors.27_report">
       </span>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Auditors'_report">
        Auditors' report
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Auditors' report">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <p>
       The board of experts designated at the 13 June session, by committee president Raimundo Lira, was heard on 5 July. This board had audited the documents, as requested by the defense and authorized by Lewandowski. They found that the delays in the transfer of payments to the public banks did indeed constitute loans. However, they avoided considering whether the President intended this and said that this judgement should be made by the senators. Also heard were the assistant to the prosecution, Selene Péres Nunes and the assistant to the defense, Ricardo Lodi Ribeiro. Nunes said that there was willful misconduct by the President, since the operations had been concealed via the accounting and the fact that the government had later issued a
       <a href="/wiki/Provisional_measure" title="Provisional measure">
        provisional measure
       </a>
       allowing payment of the debts.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147">
        <a href="#cite_note-147">
         [147]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Ribeiro said that the supplemental budget decrees were submitted for her signature by the technical departments of the ministries, and her participation, as demonstrated in the report, was limited to signing them.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148">
        <a href="#cite_note-148">
         [148]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Rousseff_interrogatory_and_final_arguments">
        Rousseff interrogatory and final arguments
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Rousseff interrogatory and final arguments">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <p>
       Rousseff was scheduled to be questioned on 6 July, but she declined to attend and sent a letter that was read by Cardozo.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149">
        <a href="#cite_note-149">
         [149]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Rousseff defended herself, claiming that she was the victim of a conspiracy—that "a number of political forces" saw her as a risk and that those who "failed to acknowledge the opposition's defeat [in the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brazilian_general_elections,_2014" title="Brazilian general elections, 2014">
        2014 elections
       </a>
       ]" wanted a different political party for the country. She also said she acted in
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bona_fide" title="Bona fide">
         bona fide
        </a>
       </i>
       and asked lawmakers to "get rid of personal bias".
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150">
        <a href="#cite_note-150">
         [150]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The final arguments were delivered on 12 July
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151">
        <a href="#cite_note-151">
         [151]
        </a>
       </sup>
       and 28 July
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152">
        <a href="#cite_note-152">
         [152]
        </a>
       </sup>
       respectively, for preparation of the final report by rapporteur Antonio Anastasia.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153">
        <a href="#cite_note-153">
         [153]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Final_report:_discussion_and_approval">
        Final report: discussion and approval
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Final report: discussion and approval">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <p>
       Anastasia submitted the final report on 2 August,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154">
        <a href="#cite_note-154">
         [154]
        </a>
       </sup>
       concluding that Rousseff was culpable.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155">
        <a href="#cite_note-155">
         [155]
        </a>
       </sup>
       On 3 August, the document was discussed by the committee. João Correia Serra, prosecution lawyer
       <i>
        in lieu
       </i>
       ,
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify">
          <span title="The text near this tag may need clarification or removal of jargon. (April 2017)">
           clarification needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
       praised Anastasia's report and stressed the known "centralizing temperament" of Rousseff, making it seem unlikely Rousseff had been unaware of or had not directly ordered the actions of which she was accused. Countering, Cardozo said that he was sure that Anastasia's report did not evince that Rousseff had committed crimes, and accused the
       <i>
        rapporteur
       </i>
       , despite his aptitude and brilliance, of managing his actions within the opinion of his party.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156">
        <a href="#cite_note-156">
         [156]
        </a>
       </sup>
       On 4 August, the report was voted on and approved by 14–5 votes – ending the work of the Committee – followed by voting on the Senate floor on 9 August, chaired by Supreme Federal Court president Ricardo Lewandowski.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-157">
        <a href="#cite_note-157">
         [157]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-158">
        <a href="#cite_note-158">
         [158]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Senate_vote_on_the_final_report">
        Senate vote on the final report
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Senate vote on the final report">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       At a long session of the Senate – from 9 to 10 August – Anastasia's final report was approved
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-159">
        <a href="#cite_note-159">
         [159]
        </a>
       </sup>
       and by a 59–21 vote, the indictments against Rousseff were upheld.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-160">
        <a href="#cite_note-160">
         [160]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-161">
        <a href="#cite_note-161">
         [161]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-162">
        <a href="#cite_note-162">
         [162]
        </a>
       </sup>
       This marked the end of the penultimate phase of the impeachment process, called
       <i>
        pronunciation
       </i>
       , which would determine the final judgement in the Senate, beginning on 25 August. In this judgement, two-thirds of 81 senators were necessary to remove the President and make her ineligible for office for another eight years with effect from 1 January 2019, when her second term would have ended.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163">
        <a href="#cite_note-163">
         [163]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Deciding_Senate_vote">
        Deciding Senate vote
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Deciding Senate vote">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The last phase of the trial consisted of four steps:
      </p>
      <ol>
       <li>
        Cross-examination of witnesses by Lewandowski and the senators (eight witnesses, two called by the prosecution and six by the defense), followed by cross-examination by prosecution and defense lawyers.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164">
         <a href="#cite_note-164">
          [164]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        Cross-examination of Rousseff by senators,
       </li>
       <li>
        Final arguments by prosecution and defense.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-165">
         <a href="#cite_note-165">
          [165]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        Vote by senators.
       </li>
      </ol>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Cross-examination_of_witnesses">
        Cross-examination of witnesses
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Cross-examination of witnesses">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <p>
       On 25 August, the prosecution called two witnesses, Julio Marcelo de Oliveira, procurator of the TCU, and author of the report recommending the rejection of the 2014 accounts, and Antonio Carlos Costa D'avila Carvalho Júnior, auditor of the TCU. Oliveira was questioned as an expert, not as an evidentiary, witness, as ruled by Lewandowski, after Cardozo accused Oliveira of making a report based on a biased understanding. He denied this, saying that he only fulfilled a recommendation to adopt a "less tolerant" rule that came from TCU. Oliveira asserted that Rousseff broke budget laws in 2014 and also in 2015. In his status as informant, his complaints could not be considered as evidence, but as technical information.
      </p>
      <p>
       The next prosecution witness questioned, D'Avila Carvalho, asserted that Rousseff "disguised" the accounting and was responsible for delaying transfers to state banks. Cardozo tried to disqualify this witness, accusing him of bias because he had helped Oliveira to draft the TCU report, "clearly an unethical situation that violates the principle of impartiality." However, Lewandowski overruled this motion.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-166">
        <a href="#cite_note-166">
         [166]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div class="thumb tleft">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Come%C3%A7a_o_julgamento_de_Dilma_Rousseff_no_Senado_1040095-df_25.08.2016_mcag-2928.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2533" data-file-width="3800" height="200" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/Come%C3%A7a_o_julgamento_de_Dilma_Rousseff_no_Senado_1040095-df_25.08.2016_mcag-2928.jpg/300px-Come%C3%A7a_o_julgamento_de_Dilma_Rousseff_no_Senado_1040095-df_25.08.2016_mcag-2928.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/Come%C3%A7a_o_julgamento_de_Dilma_Rousseff_no_Senado_1040095-df_25.08.2016_mcag-2928.jpg/450px-Come%C3%A7a_o_julgamento_de_Dilma_Rousseff_no_Senado_1040095-df_25.08.2016_mcag-2928.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/Come%C3%A7a_o_julgamento_de_Dilma_Rousseff_no_Senado_1040095-df_25.08.2016_mcag-2928.jpg/600px-Come%C3%A7a_o_julgamento_de_Dilma_Rousseff_no_Senado_1040095-df_25.08.2016_mcag-2928.jpg 2x" width="300"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Come%C3%A7a_o_julgamento_de_Dilma_Rousseff_no_Senado_1040095-df_25.08.2016_mcag-2928.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <center>
          Impeachment trial begins on 25 August 2016
         </center>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Cross-examination continued the next day when the defense called six witnesses:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Luiz_Gonzaga_Belluzzo&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Luiz Gonzaga Belluzzo (page does not exist)">
         Luiz Gonzaga Belluzzo
        </a>
        <span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">
         (
         <a class="extiw" href="https://pt.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luiz_Gonzaga_Belluzzo" title="pt:Luiz Gonzaga Belluzzo">
          pt
         </a>
         )
        </span>
        , economist,
       </li>
       <li>
        Geraldo Luiz Mascarenhas Prado, legal advisor,
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Luiz_Cl%C3%A1udio_Costa&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Luiz Cláudio Costa (page does not exist)">
         Luiz Cláudio Costa
        </a>
        <span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">
         (
         <a class="extiw" href="https://pt.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luiz_Cl%C3%A1udio_Costa" title="pt:Luiz Cláudio Costa">
          pt
         </a>
         )
        </span>
        , former Secretary of the
        <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Education_(Brazil)" title="Ministry of Education (Brazil)">
         Ministry of Education
        </a>
        ,
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Nelson_Barbosa" title="Nelson Barbosa">
         Nelson Barbosa
        </a>
        , former
        <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Planning,_Budget,_and_Management" title="Ministry of Planning, Budget, and Management">
         Minister of Planning, Budget and Management
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Esther Dweck, former Secretary of Federal Budget
       </li>
       <li>
        Ricardo Ribeiro Lodi, Law professor at the
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/State_University_of_Rio_de_Janeiro" title="State University of Rio de Janeiro">
         State University of Rio de Janeiro
        </a>
        .
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Dweck was found by Lewandowski to have a conflict of interest, since she was being contracted for the office of
       <a href="/wiki/Gleisi_Hoffmann" title="Gleisi Hoffmann">
        Gleisi Hoffmann
       </a>
       , one of the senators opposed to impeachment. Gonzaga Belluzzo and Ribeiro Lodi testified as
       <a href="/wiki/Expert_witness" title="Expert witness">
        expert witnesses
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-167">
        <a href="#cite_note-167">
         [167]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Belluzo said that removal of an elected official should require very special care and could only be done in extreme situations, and that the trial wasn't facing one.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-168">
        <a href="#cite_note-168">
         [168]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Mascarenhas Prado said that in signing decrees Rousseff had relied on subordinates who vouched for the signings' legality, adding that she "was dismissed for issuing a decree to follow a determination of the National Justice Council".
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169">
        <a href="#cite_note-169">
         [169]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Cláudio Costa said the supplementary credit decrees were used for educational programs. Senator
       <a href="/wiki/C%C3%A1ssio_Cunha_Lima" title="Cássio Cunha Lima">
        Cássio Cunha Lima
       </a>
       refuted this, stating that the crime was not in the expansion of universities and technical schools, but in the lack of congressional authorization for the decrees.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-170">
        <a href="#cite_note-170">
         [170]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Barbosa said that decrees provide more leeway for the administration of funds when the budget is limited, and are used by experienced officials. Pro-impeachment senators insisted that the decrees had aggravated the economic crisis facing the country. Barbosa countered that the crisis was due to various internal and external factors.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-171">
        <a href="#cite_note-171">
         [171]
        </a>
       </sup>
       At last, Ribeiro Lodi stated that the decrees issued by the President in July and August 2015 were not, until the time of the trial, considered violations by TCU and that when they were issued, current understanding did not exist.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-172">
        <a href="#cite_note-172">
         [172]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Cross-examination_of_Rousseff_by_senators_and_final_arguments_by_lawyers">
        Cross-examination of Rousseff by senators and final arguments by lawyers
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Cross-examination of Rousseff by senators and final arguments by lawyers">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">
       <tr>
        <td class="mbox-image">
         <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg">
          <img alt="[icon]" data-file-height="31" data-file-width="44" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" width="20"/>
         </a>
        </td>
        <td class="mbox-text">
         <div class="mbox-text-span">
          <b>
           This section needs expansion
          </b>
          .
          <small>
           You can help by
           <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=">
            adding to it
           </a>
           .
          </small>
          <small>
           <i>
            (August 2016)
           </i>
          </small>
         </div>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <table class="cquote pullquote" role="presentation" style="float:right; border-collapse: collapse; border: none; background-color: transparent; width: 22%;">
       <tr>
        <td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: top; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: left; padding: 10px 10px;">
         “
        </td>
        <td style="vertical-align: top; border: none; padding: 4px 10px;">
         <small>
          I know I will be judged, but my conscience is clear. I did not commit a crime.
         </small>
        </td>
        <td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: bottom; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: right; padding: 10px 10px;">
         ”
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td class="cquotecite" colspan="3" style="border: none; padding-right: 4%; font-size: smaller; text-align: right;">
         <cite>
          — Dilma Rousseff,
          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-def_173-0">
           <a href="#cite_note-def-173">
            [173]
           </a>
          </sup>
         </cite>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Discurso_no_Senado_Federal_(29282582566).jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2211" data-file-width="3506" height="189" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/Discurso_no_Senado_Federal_%2829282582566%29.jpg/300px-Discurso_no_Senado_Federal_%2829282582566%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/Discurso_no_Senado_Federal_%2829282582566%29.jpg/450px-Discurso_no_Senado_Federal_%2829282582566%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/Discurso_no_Senado_Federal_%2829282582566%29.jpg/600px-Discurso_no_Senado_Federal_%2829282582566%29.jpg 2x" width="300"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Discurso_no_Senado_Federal_(29282582566).jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <center>
          Dilma Rousseff at the Senate on 29 August 2016
         </center>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Rousseff spoke in her own defense before the Senate on 29 August for 45 minutes, proclaiming her innocence and decrying the impeachment process, noting that many of her accusers faced worse charges than she.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LA_76-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-LA-76">
         [76]
        </a>
       </sup>
       "Everybody knows this impeachment process opened with explicit blackmail by the former head of the lower house, Eduardo Cunha,”
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-174">
        <a href="#cite_note-174">
         [174]
        </a>
       </sup>
       she said. She then answered questions from senators for more than twelve hours.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-175">
        <a href="#cite_note-175">
         [175]
        </a>
       </sup>
       She explained that she had needed to make difficult choices on the budget, to address declining
       <a href="/wiki/Revenue" title="Revenue">
        revenue
       </a>
       and a refusal by opposition in Congress to work with her.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-def_173-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-def-173">
         [173]
        </a>
       </sup>
       She compared her situation with other Brazilian presidents pursued by their opponents, including
       <a href="/wiki/Jo%C3%A3o_Goulart" title="João Goulart">
        João Goulart
       </a>
       , a leftist ousted in a
       <a href="/wiki/1964_Brazilian_coup_d%27%C3%A9tat" title="1964 Brazilian coup d'état">
        military coup in 1964
       </a>
       , and replaced by a 21-year dictatorship.
      </p>
      <p>
       She also compared the effort to impeach her to the torture she endured after agents of the military dictatorship arrested and jailed her as an
       <a href="/wiki/Dilma_Rousseff#Guerrilla_activity,_1968–69" title="Dilma Rousseff">
        urban guerrilla
       </a>
       . Rousseff called the impeachment proceedings a new type of coup and evoked the breakdown of Brazilian democracy in the 1960s before the military coup. Senator
       <a href="/wiki/Ana_Am%C3%A9lia_Lemos" title="Ana Amélia Lemos">
        Ana Amélia Lemos
       </a>
       in reply expressed respect for her personal history but said that the senators were not there to judge her biography, but the actions of her government. She said Rousseff had broken the law by manipulating the budget to hide economic problems.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-176">
        <a href="#cite_note-176">
         [176]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <table class="cquote pullquote" role="presentation" style="float:right; border-collapse: collapse; border: none; background-color: transparent; width: 18%;">
       <tr>
        <td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: top; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: left; padding: 10px 10px;">
         “
        </td>
        <td style="vertical-align: top; border: none; padding: 4px 10px;">
         <small>
          We are not dealing with a little accounting problem; we are dealing with fraud.
         </small>
        </td>
        <td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: bottom; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: right; padding: 10px 10px;">
         ”
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td class="cquotecite" colspan="3" style="border: none; padding-right: 4%; font-size: smaller; text-align: right;">
         <cite>
          — Janaína Paschoal,
          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-def_173-2">
           <a href="#cite_note-def-173">
            [173]
           </a>
          </sup>
         </cite>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <p>
       The proceedings resumed on 30 August with final arguments of the prosecution and defense,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-177">
        <a href="#cite_note-177">
         [177]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-178">
        <a href="#cite_note-178">
         [178]
        </a>
       </sup>
       followed by speeches from the senators—the speeches lasted twelve hours, ending about 02:30
       <span class="nowrap">
       </span>
       am on the 31st.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-179">
        <a href="#cite_note-179">
         [179]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Senate_vote">
        Senate vote
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Senate vote">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <p>
       The Senate found President Dilma Rousseff guilty of responsibility crimes and administrative misconduct regarding the federal budget and removed her from office after a vote of 61–20 on 31 August 2016.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto_8-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto-8">
         [8]
        </a>
       </sup>
       In a separate vote on whether she should be barred from public office for eight years, senators voted 42-36 in favor. A two-thirds majority of the votes (54 of 81 senators) would have been needed, so she will be able to run for any public office again in the near future.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-180">
        <a href="#cite_note-180">
         [180]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-181">
        <a href="#cite_note-181">
         [181]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-182">
        <a href="#cite_note-182">
         [182]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-183">
        <a href="#cite_note-183">
         [183]
        </a>
       </sup>
       She has vowed to do so.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-184">
        <a href="#cite_note-184">
         [184]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <table class="wikitable plainrowheaders sortable" style="font-size:100%; text-align:right;">

      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Lawsuits_against_the_Senate_judgment">
        Lawsuits against the Senate judgment
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Lawsuits against the Senate judgment">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <p>
       Rousseff's defense on 1 September 2016 filed a
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Writ_of_mandamus" title="Writ of mandamus">
        writ of mandamus
       </a>
       with the Supreme Court against the Senate decision to remove her from office,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-187">
        <a href="#cite_note-187">
         [187]
        </a>
       </sup>
       which the court rejected on 8 September.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-188">
        <a href="#cite_note-188">
         [188]
        </a>
       </sup>
       On 30 September, the defense filed a last appeal of the impeachment. A 493-page piece called for an annulment. "
       <i>
        This petition is aimed at invalidating the decision-making legal act of the Senate that led to the conviction, on August 31 this year, for the crime of responsibility of Her Excellency President of the Republic, Dilma Rousseff
       </i>
       ", reads the text.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-189">
        <a href="#cite_note-189">
         [189]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The appeal, signed by José Eduardo Cardozo, was denied by the Supreme Court on 20 October.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-190">
        <a href="#cite_note-190">
         [190]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       On the other hand, the parties PSDB,
       <a href="/wiki/Democrats_(Brazil)" title="Democrats (Brazil)">
        DEM
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Popular_Socialist_Party_(Brazil)" title="Popular Socialist Party (Brazil)">
        PPS
       </a>
       also decided to file a
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Mandamus" title="Mandamus">
         mandamus
        </a>
       </i>
       at the Supreme Court against the Senate's decision to vote separately on the loss of political rights during the impeachment trial, thereby allowing the former President to later run for public office, as opposed to the laws defining crimes of responsibility and regulating the respective trial process (
       <i>
        impeachment law
       </i>
       ),
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-191">
        <a href="#cite_note-191">
         [191]
        </a>
       </sup>
       that determines a concommitance of penalties.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-192">
        <a href="#cite_note-192">
         [192]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="After_impeachment">
        After impeachment
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: After impeachment">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">
       <tr>
        <td class="mbox-image">
         <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg">
          <img alt="[icon]" data-file-height="31" data-file-width="44" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" width="20"/>
         </a>
        </td>
        <td class="mbox-text">
         <div class="mbox-text-span">
          <b>
           This section needs expansion
          </b>
          .
          <small>
           You can help by
           <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=">
            adding to it
           </a>
           .
          </small>
          <small>
           <i>
            (September 2016)
           </i>
          </small>
         </div>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Reactions">
        Reactions
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Reactions">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="International_reaction">
        International reaction
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: International reaction">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <p>
       In May 2016, just after Senate voted to suspend Rousseff's presidential powers. A
       <a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">
        <i>
         New York Times
        </i>
       </a>
       editorial voiced support for Rousseff's concerns about the integrity and possible ulterior motives of the politicians who voted for her impeachment, though it considered her defense "debatable".
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nyted_193-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nyted-193">
         [193]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The
       <a href="/wiki/Union_of_South_American_Nations" title="Union of South American Nations">
        South American
       </a>
       countries of
       <a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">
        Ecuador
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">
        Bolivia
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">
        Venezuela
       </a>
       reacted to the impeachment of the President by recalling their ambassadors.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-194">
        <a href="#cite_note-194">
         [194]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The government of
       <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">
        Argentina
       </a>
       declared neutrality, viewing the impeachment as an internal Brazilian affair;
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-195">
        <a href="#cite_note-195">
         [195]
        </a>
       </sup>
       the Argentine Ministry of Foreign Affairs said that they recognized "the institutional process" that had taken place.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-196">
        <a href="#cite_note-196">
         [196]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Representatives from Bolivia, Costa Rica, Cuba, Ecuador, Nicaragua and Venezuela walked out during Temer's speech at the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UN_General_Assembly" title="UN General Assembly">
        UN General Assembly
       </a>
       on 20 September 2016.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-197">
        <a href="#cite_note-197">
         [197]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Temer defended the impeachment, and said that it occurred with "absolute respect for the constitutional order".
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-198">
        <a href="#cite_note-198">
         [198]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       On 22 August, about a week before the impeachment vote, the Brazilian Senate submitted a letter to the
       <a href="/wiki/Organization_of_American_States" title="Organization of American States">
        Organization of American States
       </a>
       (OAS) in response to a complaint from PT, that the impeachment process was an "institutional coup". OAS asked for information about this complaint and the Brazilian Senate stated in the letter that "the constitutional rules were strictly observed, objections raised, and appeals to the Supreme Court were accepted."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-199">
        <a href="#cite_note-199">
         [199]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       In a press release in early September, just after the final vote, the
       <a href="/wiki/Inter-American_Commission_on_Human_Rights" title="Inter-American Commission on Human Rights">
        Inter-American Commission on Human Rights
       </a>
       of OAS expressed concern about the impeachment procedure.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-200">
        <a href="#cite_note-200">
         [200]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="National_reaction">
        National reaction
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: National reaction">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <p>
       The television coverage of the impeachment vote on 31 August 2016, was watched by 35.1 million viewers in Brazil, according to
       <a href="/wiki/GfK" title="GfK">
        GfK
       </a>
       research.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-201">
        <a href="#cite_note-201">
         [201]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       After the decision of the Senate to impeach Rousseff, protests organized by supporters of the former president took place in several Brazilian cities against the decision and calling for new elections.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-202">
        <a href="#cite_note-202">
         [202]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-203">
        <a href="#cite_note-203">
         [203]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-204">
        <a href="#cite_note-204">
         [204]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Public_opinion_survey_and_economics">
        Public opinion survey and economics
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Impeachment_of_Dilma_Rousseff&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Public opinion survey and economics">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       In an
       <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Institute_of_Public_Opinion_and_Statistics" title="Brazilian Institute of Public Opinion and Statistics">
        Ibope
       </a>
       survey in September, after approximately a month of President Temer's administration, 39% of Brazilians rated his administration "bad or terrible", while 14% considered it "great or good". 2,002 people were heard between 20 and 25 September, and the margin of error was two percentage points.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-205">
        <a href="#cite_note-205">
         [205]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The Brazilian
       <a href="/wiki/%C3%8Dndice_Bovespa" title="Índice Bovespa">
        Bovespa stock index
       </a>
       (.BVSP) gained more than 20% in 2016.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-206">
        <a href="#cite_note-206">
         [206]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>

         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
          <b>
           <a href="#cite_ref-Terra_49-0">
            ^
           </a>
          </b>
         </span>
         <span class="reference-text">
          <cite class="citation web">
           <a class="external text" href="http://noticias.terra.com.br/brasil/politica/impeachment/impeachment-dependera-do-futuro-de-cunha-na-camara-dizem-cientistas-politicos,4693873b8bb811e15bb298eaea0a3fecd25v5z3i.html" rel="nofollow">
            "Para especialistas, impeachment dependerá do futuro de Cunha"
           </a>
           [For experts, impeachment depends on the future of Cunha] (in Portuguese).
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Terra_Networks" title="Terra Networks">
            Terra Networks
           </a>
           . 6 December 2015
           <span class="reference-accessdate">
            . Retrieved
            <span class="nowrap">
             2 July
            </span>
            2016
           </span>
           .
           <q>
            De acordo com o professor da
            <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Universidade_Federal_de_Minas_Gerais" title="Universidade Federal de Minas Gerais">
             Universidade Federal de Minas Gerais
            </a>
            (UFMG) Leonardo Avritzer, desde a posse de Dilma, prevalece um cenário de “fragmentação política”, com demonstrada dificuldade do governo de obter apoio no Congresso Nacional. Ele atribui o problema à pouca habilidade da presidente em conquistar aliados e também a falhas no sistema político, que permite uma pulverização de partidos, tornando mais difícil a governabilidade.[...] A análise é semelhante à do vice-diretor do Instituto de Estudos Sociais e Políticos da
            <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro_State_University" title="Rio de Janeiro State University">
             Rio de Janeiro State University
            </a>
            (Uerj), João Feres Júnior. [...} Feres Júnior lembra que, desde a posse da presidente, a oposição, liderada pelo PSDB, tenta revogar o resultado das urnas. “A primeira estratégia foi pedir a recontagem de votos, alegando fraude eleitoral, depois, reprovar as contas da campanha”, cita. “A oposição está mais interessada em desestabilizar o governo e tirar a presidente do que promover o bem público”, diz /
            <b>
             Translated
            </b>
            :
            <i>
             According to Leonardo Avritzer, a professor at the
             <a href="/wiki/Federal_University_of_Minas_Gerais" title="Federal University of Minas Gerais">
              Federal University of Minas Gerais
             </a>
             (UFMG), since Dilma's inauguration, a scenario of "political fragmentation" prevails, with demonstrated difficulty for the government to obtain support in the Congress. He attributes the problem to the president's poor ability to win allies and also to failures of the political system, which allows a splintering of parties, making governance more difficult.
            </i>
            [...] "The analysis is similar to that of the deputy director of the Institute of Social and Political Studies of the
            <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/State_University_of_Rio_de_Janeiro" title="State University of Rio de Janeiro">
             State University of Rio de Janeiro
            </a>
            (Uerj), João Feres Júnior." [...]
            <i>
             Feres Júnior remember that since the president's inauguration, the opposition, led by the PSDB, had tried to revoke the result of the polls. "The first strategy was to ask for a recount, alleging electoral fraud, then, to reprove the accounts of the campaign, he cites
            </i>
            . "The opposition is more interested in destabilizing the government and removing the president; than promoting the public wellness," he says.
           </q>

        <li id="cite_note-66">
         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
          <b>
           <a href="#cite_ref-66">
            ^
           </a>
          </b>
         </span>
         <span class="reference-text">
          Request for impeachment, pg 22–38; pg.38:
          <i>
           Com efeito, como evidenciado em sede de Representação Criminal encaminhada à Procuradoria Geral da República, ao fazer empréstimos proibidos e não os contabilizar, a Presidente da República poderia até, em tese, ser inclusa nas iras do artigo 299 do Código Penal, que tipifica a falsidade ideológica. A situação resta ainda mais grave, quando se constata que todo esse expediente fora intensificado durante o ano eleitoral, com o fim deliberado de iludir o eleitorado. Daí ser possível falar em verdadeiro estelionato eleitoral.
          </i>
          <br/>
          (
          <i>
           In fact, as evidenced by a Criminal Representation sent to the Office of the Attorney General, by illegally taking loans and not accounting for them, the [actions of the] President could, in theory, be included under Article 299 of the Penal Code, which typifies identity fraud. The situation is even more serious if one observes that this procedure was intensified during election year, with the deliberate purpose of deceiving the electorate. Hence it is possible to talk about electoral fraud.
          </i>
          ) See talk page for translation discussion.

          <span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Lei+n%C2%BA+1.079%2C+de+10+de+Abril+de+1950&amp;rft.pub=Presid%C3%AAncia+da+Rep%C3%BAblica+do+Brasil&amp;rft.date=1950-04-10&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.planalto.gov.br%2Fccivil_03%2Fleis%2FL1079.htm&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AImpeachment+of+Dilma+Rousseff">
           <span style="display:none;">

           Art. 2º: The crimes defined in this law, even when simply tempted, are punishable by loss of office with disqualification, up to five years for the exercise of any public office imposed by the Senate in the cases against the President or Ministers of State, against the Justices of the Supreme Court or against the Attorney General.
